[30;1m834 | [0m[35m3. Reports are `IssuesReport` objects, as defined in the `issues_report.py`.  Reports group and[0m
[30;1m835 | [0m[35m   sort records to provide a useful structure for human-readable output formats like Word and HTML.[0m
[30;1m836 | [0m[35m   The report can be obtained from the `SarifFileSet`, `SarifFile` or `SarifRun` via the[0m
[30;1m837 | [0m[35m   `get_report()` method.[0m
[30;1m838 | [0m[35m[0m
